Score689
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 689, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 12. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

solos: Score 64. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 110

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 87 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 23 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 30 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue focusableOperable

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 58

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focOp, score 56 (Operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 44

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 42 (Non-underlined adjacent links)
  • Package axe, test link-in-text-block, score 1 (Link is not distinct from surrounding text without reliance on color)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 34

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r83, score 16 (Overflow is hidden or clipped if the text is enlarged)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 26 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue svgImageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 34

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 123, score 32 (svg element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 31

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 29 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Score: 26
